   <div class="section ahi">
    <div class="container-fluid">
     <div class="row heading">
      <div class="col flex-center">
       <h2 class="htxt">
        Exploring Heartland
       </h2>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="row content p-0">
      <div class="col-lg-4 p-0">
       <div class="bkg-tile img-hist">
        <div class="infoBox">
         <div class="w-100">
          <h3>
           Our History
          </h3>
          <div class="w-100">
           <p>
            Heartland RVs was founded in 2003 by a group of RV veterans intent on redefining RV manufacturing. Landmark, our innovative, high-end 5th wheel with innovative features, was the first to roll off the assembly line and remains one of our best-selling brands. In just 5 years we developed some of the most popular towables on the market and became a top manufacturer of 5th wheels and travel trailers - a reputation that holds true to this day.
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
         <a class="btn btn-dark mt-sm-0 mt-4" href="https://heartlandrvs.com/history/">
          Learn More
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="col-lg-4 p-0">
       <div class="bkg-tile img-lifestyle">
        <div class="infoBox">
         <div class="w-100">
          <h3>
           Experience Heartland
          </h3>
          <p>
           Want to embark on an RV adventure? You've come to the right place. We invite you to explore our lineup of popular fifth wheels, toy haulers, and travel trailers. If you're planning to RV full-time, check out Landmark, Big Country, or Bighorn. Have a motorcycle or side-by-side you want to take along? Road Warrior or Cyclone might be right for you. Need a camper for weekend trips? We have a variety of quality travel trailers from the luxurious North Trail to the retro Terry Classic.
          </p>

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
		$('.dropdown-menu a.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function(e){
			var $el = $(this);
			var $wh = $(window).height();

			var $parent = $(this).offsetParent(".dropdown-menu");
			if(!$(this).next().hasClass('show')){
				$(this).parents('.dropdown-menu').first().find('.show').removeClass("show");
			}
			var $subMenu = $(this).next(".dropdown-menu");
			$subMenu.toggleClass('show');
			$(this).parent("li").toggleClass('show');
			$(this).parents('li.nav-item.dropdown.show').on('hidden.bs.dropdown', function(e){
				$('.dropdown-menu .show' ).removeClass( "show" );
			});
			if (!$parent.parent().hasClass('navbar-nav')){
				if($el.next().hasClass('librev')){
					$el.next().css( { "top": $el[0].offsetTop, "right": $parent.outerWidth() - 4, "left": "auto"});
				} else {
					$el.next().css( { "top": $el[0].offsetTop, "left": $parent.outerWidth() - 4});
				}
			}
			return false;
		} );
	} );
  </script>
  <script>
   $(function(){
				$(window).on('resize load',resizeOwl);
				$('#fullpage').fullpage({
					verticalCentered:false,
					anchors: ['top','featured-models','about-heart','construction','customers','testimonials'],
					menu: '#sideMenu',
					animateAnchor:false,
					responsiveWidth: 991,
					responsiveHeight: 769,
					afterRender: function(){
						$('.owl-featRV').owlCarousel({loop:!0,nav:!0,items:1,navText:['<img src="images/prev2.png">','<img src="images/next2.png">']});
						$('.owl-mobile-hp').owlCarousel({items:1,loop:!0,autoplay:!0,dots:!1,lazyLoad:!0});
						$('.owl-test').owlCarousel({
							loop:true, margin:16, dotsEach:true, nav:true,stagePadding:10, margin:40, navText:['<img src="images/prev2.png">','<img src="images/next2.png">'], responsive:{
								0:{items:1},576:{items:1},992:{items:2},1200:{items:3}
							},
							onInitialized:resizeOwl
						});
					}
				});
			});
			function resizeOwl(e){
				var wh = $(window).height();
				var ww = $(window).width();
				$('owl-featRV > .item').each(function(i,v){
					767<ww?$(this).height(wh-246):$(this).height(wh-166)
					//-3rem (48px ea) - 150px header from device height OR 70px on smaller devices
				});
				$('.owl-carousel .owl-item img.owl-featRV-img').each(function(i,v){
					ww>wh?$(this).css({height:wh/2,width:'auto'}):$(this).css({'max-height':'200px',height:'auto'})
				});
			}
  </script>
